(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )
  
  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action UseObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect nil
  )

  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect nil
  )

  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect nil
  )

  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect nil
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action UseObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

  (:objects

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action UseObject
    :parameters (?o - object)
    :precondition (holding ?o)
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action HeatObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action CleanObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action CoolObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?o))
    :effect (and)
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)

    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

    :parameters (?r - receptacle)

    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

  (:action SliceObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle ?co - object ?sharp_o - object)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (holding ?sharp_o) (sharp ?sharp_o) (contains ?r ?co))
    :effect (not (contains ?r ?co))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

    (sharp ?o - object)

  )

    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)

    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject

    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  )

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

This is previous domain file: 
(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)

(define (domain textworld)
  (:requirements :strips :negative-preconditions)
  (:types receptacle object)
  (:predicates
    (at ?r - receptacle)
    (opened ?r - receptacle)
    (contains ?r - receptacle ?o - object)
    (holding ?o - object)
    (sharp ?o - object)
  )

  (:action GotoLocation
    :parameters (?from - receptacle ?to - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?from) (not (at ?to)))
    :effect (and (not (at ?from)) (at ?to))
  )

  (:action OpenObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (not (opened ?r)))
    :effect (opened ?r)
  )

  (:action CloseObject
    :parameters (?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r))
    :effect (not (opened ?r))
  )

  (:action PickupObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (contains ?r ?o) (not (holding ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (contains ?r ?o)) (holding ?o))
  )

  (:action PutObject
    :parameters (?o - object ?r - receptacle)
    :precondition (and (at ?r) (opened ?r) (holding ?o) (not (contains ?r ?o)))
    :effect (and (not (holding ?o)) (contains ?r ?o))
  )
)
